Provide a short reasoning before deciding.

[planner_qa_rationale_imaginator] **Reasoning**  
The agent is already at (3.0, 0.0). The cucumber is at (3.5, 1.5) and the table at (3.5, 0.5). A shortest sequence is:

1. Move east to the x‑coordinate of both objects.  
2. Move north to the cucumber’s tile, take it.  
3. Move south to the table’s tile and drop it.

No other objects or doors need to be considered, so this plan is still promising and minimal.

**Action sequence**

1. `move` from **(3.0, 0.0)** → **(3.5, 0.0)**
2. `move` from **(3.5, 0.0)** → **(3.5, 1.5)**
3. `take cucumber_3`
4. `move` from **(3.5, 1.5)** → **(3.5, 0.5)**
5. `drop cucumber_3`
